| 1:02:40| We also, in the Black community, recognize New Year's.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-201221?start=3760)|
| 1:02:45| Of course, for many, New Year's, January 1,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-201221?start=3765)|
| 1:02:48| is a time where folks gather together and celebrate with libations or house parties.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-201221?start=3768)|
| 1:02:55| But within the Black church tradition, we gather on New Year's Eve, going into New Year's,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-201221?start=3775)|
| 1:03:05| what we call Watch Night, which commemorates and celebrates the anticipation| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-201221?start=3785)|
